  )\n339\t        reasons = []\n340\t        if delta <= tolerance:\n341\t            reasons.append(\"no positive coupling to the active lost distinction\")\n342\t        if not math.isclose(delta, row[\"negativity\"] > 1e-12 for row in train\n73\t    )\n74\t\n75\t    def nearest_lookup(row: dict[str, float]) -> float:\n76\t        nearest = min(train, key=lambda item: abs(item[\"angle\"] -
